Who We Are

Two Js.
One Vision.

Double J was founded by Jake and Jay — two partners united by a shared commitment to quality craftsmanship and responsible development. We treat every project as if it were our own.

From ground-up development and general contracting to full-service property management, we're with you at every stage.

What We Do

Our Services

From concept to completion — and beyond. A full suite of real estate services under one roof.

01

Development

We turn raw land and bold ideas into viable real estate projects — managing feasibility, entitlements, design coordination, and execution.

  • Site Selection & Feasibility
  • Land Acquisition
  • Project Planning & Design
  • Permit & Entitlement Management
02

Construction

Quality-first general contracting for commercial builds. Every detail managed so your project lands on time and on budget.

  • New Construction
  • Commercial Buildouts
  • Quality Control & Inspections
03

Property Management

Protect and grow your investment with professional property management. We handle tenant relations, maintenance, and reporting.

  • Tenant Screening
  • Rent Collection
  • Maintenance Coordination
  • Financial Reporting
04

Relationships

We don't just build structures — we build partnerships. Every client we work with becomes a long-term relationship. We stay accessible, communicate honestly, and show up the same way on day one as we do on day one hundred.

  • Transparent Communication
  • Long-Term Client Partnerships
  • Honest Timelines & Budgets
  • Post-Project Support

Double J is built on a simple idea: two people who care deeply about what they build and stand behind every project they touch. Jake and Jay bring complementary skills and a shared work ethic that sets the tone for everything Double J does.

Jake

Co-Founder · Development

Jake leads development and strategy at Double J. He stays involved from the very beginning — working through site selection, land acquisition, and design coordination — and stays in it all the way to the end. He keeps things straightforward and makes sure every project starts the right way.

Jay

Co-Founder · Construction

Jay runs all construction operations at Double J. He oversees every build from groundbreaking to final walkthrough — managing subcontractors, timelines, and quality control to ensure every project meets the highest standards of craftsmanship, on schedule and on budget.
